    function createFallingWord() {

      // ุชูุฒูุน ุนุดูุงุฆู ุฃููู
      span.style.left = Math.random() * 100 + "vw";

      // ูุฏุฉ ุงูุณููุท ุนุดูุงุฆูุฉ ุจูู 10 ู 20 ุซุงููุฉ (ุจุทูุก)

      // ุจุฏุงูุฉ ูุชุฃุฎุฑุฉ ุนุดูุงุฆูุฉ ูุชูุฒูุน ุงูุณููุท

   // 1) ุชุฃุซูุฑ ASCII/Matrix ุงูุฎููู

   const cvs = document.getElementById('ascii');
   const ctx = cvs.getContext('2d');
   let W, H, cols, drops, glyphs;
   function size(){
     W = cvs.width = innerWidth * devicePixelRatio;
     H = cvs.height = innerHeight * devicePixelRatio;
     ctx.scale(devicePixelRatio, devicePixelRatio);
     cols = Math.floor(innerWidth / 14);
     drops = Array(cols).fill(0);
     glyphs = "^*#โชฮฮฉโโโฆโงโฃโขโโโโ".split(""); // ASCII/ุฑููุฒ ุฑูุญูุฉ
   }
   size(); addEventListener('resize', size);
   function rain(){
     ctx.fillStyle = 'rgba(0,0,0,0.08)';
     ctx.fillRect(0,0,innerWidth,innerHeight);
     for(let i=0;i<cols;i++){
       const ch = glyphs[(Math.random()*glyphs.length)|0];
       ctx.fillStyle = Math.random()<0.05? '#ffd166' : '#7bdff2';
       ctx.fillText(ch, i*14, (drops[i]*14));
       if (drops[i]*14 > innerHeight && Math.random() > 0.975) drops[i]=0; else drops[i]++;
     }
     requestAnimationFrame(rain);
   }
   ctx.font = '16px monospace';
   ctx.shadowColor = '#00ffff';
   ctx.shadowBlur = 8;
   rain();
